Italy, Austria, and Hungary Agree on the Post-Establishment Europe (Paris Correspondence) 106

The European political situation is showing significant changes. France's hegemony is gradually faltering. Aside from France, which is relatively stable, and a few countries like the Netherlands and Belgium, which have some solutions, the economic problems of the European continent are being stirred up by economic panic. In particular, Germany and the Danubian countries of Austria-Hungary are being severely shaken. In the past, four-power conferences were held in London under the guidance of France, and other conferences, such as the Lausanne Conference and the Stresa Conference, were aimed at solving the economic problems of the Danubian countries, but ultimately had no effect, instead making the problems more complex and harder to solve.

In this chaotic situation, Germany's economic situation is indeed deteriorating, reaching a point close to collapse. However, its political tone remains high, calling for the rejection of the Treaty of Versailles, demanding equal military status, and so on. At the same time, it is doing its best to stir up German patriotism, trying to form a system centered on the Germanic nation, and of course, aiming to divide the hegemony of Europe.

At this time, Italy is a country that is developing strongly, and at the same time, it is in opposition to France in Europe, in the Mediterranean, and in North Africa. It helps Germany, but does not want Germany to be too strong. Therefore, it takes advantage of this time – when Germany's strength is not yet sufficient – to first free Austria from Germany's control, and second to make Austria-Hungary inclined to Italy's leadership. As a result, this brewing was successful. On March 12, Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös arrived in Rome, and on the 13th, Austrian dictator Chancellor Dollfuss also arrived. The two met with Italy's Mussolini on the 14th at the Villa Chigi Palace in Rome. At this time, Mussolini's attitude was very clever. During the negotiations, he almost put aside political issues and focused on economics. On the 16th, the meeting yielded results, and on the 17th, their protocol was issued. The first protocol was a political statement by the three countries, which stated, "For the purpose of using existing treaties and friendly relations between the three countries as a standard, all issues, especially issues that are of interest to the three countries, or common issues, must be coordinated...for the purpose of promoting effective cooperation among the three countries..." There were two other protocols on economic issues, the content of which included, "Establishing the expansion of the current trade treaty between Italy and the other two countries, granting preferential treatment to Austrian industrial products, and based on the low price of grain, Italian and Austrian industries should reach an understanding to overcome Hungary's difficulties, and through the Adriatic Sea ports (namely, Fiume and Trieste), stipulate how to promote the transportation of goods..."

The political impact of this agreement is that, on the one hand, it completely shattered Germany's plan to annex Austria, and on the other hand, it has the intention of abrogating or amending the Treaty of Versailles, the Treaty of Trianon, and the Treaty of Saint-Germain, which has a serious relationship with the future of the European political situation. On the other hand, economically, Austria formerly had to export through Hamburg and Bremen through Germany, although the route was relatively long, it had no choice. Now that Italy has opened up the right to navigation in the Adriatic Sea to them, and Fiume and Trieste are precisely the ports that Austria and Hungary urgently want to obtain, this is Italy's foundation for establishing economic hegemony in Central Europe, and the prelude to the Central European dispute. Secondly, Italy, Austria, and Hungary have not closed the door, and also intend to attract the Danubian countries to join their organization. If this can really be formed, then the Little Entente will tend to Italy, and France's European hegemony will of course be hit, which is also very unfavorable to Germany, preventing its development.

According to the published documents, this agreement does not seem to have any intention of undermining the past international treaties, but rather wants to maintain them. However, this is ultimately a diplomatic courtesy. In practice, it still tries its best to exert its subtle skills to break the current situation in Europe, especially the League of Nations is threatened by this kind of sabotage. It cannot make Italy and the Danubian countries loyal to the League of Nations and fulfill international cooperation, nor can it promote the power of the League of Nations to pacify the inequalities of the small countries in Europe. Therefore, Germany and Italy each use their diplomatic means to win over small countries as satellites. In other words, it is to abandon the form of international conferences and turn to the struggle of vertical and horizontal alliances. (March 19, Paris)

Page 9

Tianjin City: Rioters Seize Guns and Kill People; Five Gun-Grabbing Cases Occur in One Morning, One Police Officer Killed and One Policeman Injured 107

Tianjin Correspondence: From midnight on the 24th to around 1 a.m. on the 25th, five cases of bandits robbing police officers of their firearms occurred simultaneously in the French Concession and the Nanshi district of Tianjin, and one police officer was shot and killed. Their actions seemed to be planned in advance. The bandits all fled into the Japanese Concession afterward, and spoke Japanese in a non-native accent when committing the crimes, leading some to suspect that they were plainclothes agents instigated by a certain party to deliberately disrupt Tianjin's security. The facts are described in detail below. At 0:50 a.m. on the 24th, police officer Shi Lifang of the Sixth Precinct of the First District of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, who was on duty in front of the Rong'an Street Hygiene Pond, suddenly saw two people, shabbily dressed and resembling workers, walking out of the Japanese Concession. Approaching Shi, they used a question as an excuse, and while the officer was unprepared, they grabbed him and dragged him into the Japanese Concession, taking his Mauser pistol and ordering him not to make a sound. They also ordered the officer to kneel against the wall. Officer Shi, unable to bear the insult, rose up to resist, and the two bandits struck him in the head with their gun butts, causing him to faint instantly. When Shi regained consciousness, the two bandits were gone. At that time, the road was quiet and there were few people. The officer staggered back to the station to report. Station Chief Tian Jiurong was about to lead his men out to pursue when he received a report from Patrol Captain Xue Peilu of the Fifth Outpost of the station, stating that police officer Liu Kuiqing, who was on duty on Fugui Street in the outpost, had also been shot in the chest by bandits. Tian immediately ordered him to be transported to the station. Shortly afterward, Officer Liu was carried in by people. According to [Liu], at approximately 1:20 a.m. on the 25th, two people suddenly walked out of the Japanese Concession, walked up to him, and one person suddenly grabbed Liu, while the other used force to seize the Mauser pistol Liu was wearing. Liu struggled, but the man fired the seized gun at Liu, hitting him in the chest and exiting through his back, causing him to faint immediately. The two bandits also fled immediately. After Station Chief Tian received reports of the two gun-grabbing incidents, he immediately reported by telephone to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau and dispatched police officers to search for the bandits. At this time, he received a telephone report from the Fourth Outpost of the Haiguang Temple of the station, stating that at 1:30 a.m., two bandits had walked from the direction of the Haiguang Temple and fired two shots at the outpost, but did not hit anyone. By the time the outpost chief and police officers came out with guns, the bandits were gone. These three incidents occurred simultaneously within the jurisdiction of the Sixth Police Station of the Nanshi district. After receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately ordered the Security Team to move out and patrol, and armored vehicles were sent out to patrol. Fortunately, nothing else happened afterward. Officer Shi, who was injured, was not seriously injured and is expected to recover in two or three days. Officer Liu was sent to the Municipal Hospital, and although he lost a lot of blood, he is still out of danger. The newly appointed Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Chief Li Junxiang specially allocated 30 yuan yesterday for the officer's medical expenses and granted him a one-month leave for treatment.

While the above three incidents were occurring in the Nanshi district, Hua Police Officer No. 118, in front of No. 118 Sanhuai Lane behind the church in the Tianjin French Concession, was suddenly surrounded by three bandits, each wielding handguns and sharp knives. They threatened him and seized the officer's handgun, and then fled towards Mingde Fort in front of the church. The officer chased after them, blowing his whistle to warn others. At that time, Hua Police Officer Luo Fengzhang, No. 130, who was on duty in front of the church, heard the whistle and saw someone running frantically, and went forward to intercept them. He was shot twice by the bandits, one bullet hitting his head, and because it was a vital spot, he fell to the ground immediately. At this time, Hua Police Officer No. 93, No. 37, who was on duty at the entrance of the Lubei Chen Hotel, had also heard the alarm and was about to go to assist when he suddenly saw three people walking quickly on the sidewalk, speaking Japanese. The officer immediately raised his gun and questioned them. The three replied that they were going to find someone ahead. The officer did not suspect anything and continued to chase forward, but the three bandits suddenly turned around and grabbed the officer, snatched his handgun, and ran wildly towards the Japanese Concession. At this time, Hua Police Officer No. 85, who was on duty at No. 31, was also grabbed by two bandits, who seized his handgun and fled into Suma Street in the Japanese Concession. It is said that the bandits who seized the guns were all Chinese, deliberately speaking a broken Sino-Japanese language to avoid attracting attention. After the perpetrators fled into the Japanese Concession, it seemed that someone was waiting to assist them, so the authorities are paying close attention to this matter. Hua Police Officer Luo Fengzhang, No. 130, who was injured, died at 3 p.m. today due to his serious injuries. (25th)

Taiwan Convenes a Consulate Conference on the Other Side; Taiwan Governor to Schedule Conference Immediately After Returning from Tokyo 108

Xiamen Correspondence: Xiamen and Taiwan are only a night's journey away by sea. From Magong in Taiwan to Xiamen, a destroyer can reach it in six hours. The same is true for Fuzhou. Therefore, the close relationship between Fujian and Taiwan and the large number of Japanese Taiwanese residing in Fuzhou and Xiamen form a special phenomenon. Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota recently summoned foreign ambassadors and consuls back to the country for training. The Japanese consuls in Fuzhou and Xiamen were also among those summoned. Takashi Tsukamoto, the Japanese consul in Xiamen, took the Phoenix Mountain Maru to Taiwan on April 10 and returned to Tokyo. According to recent news from Taiwan, the Governor-General of Taiwan, in view of the extremely close relationship between Taiwan and the other side, is eager to establish a policy towards South China. It has been decided to convene consuls from Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shanghai, Shantou, and Guangdong to Taiwan in late June to hold a consulate conference on the other side in the Governor-General's VIP room to discuss various important matters concerning the policy towards South China. This conference was originally scheduled to be held when the consuls from Fuzhou, Xiamen, etc. were passing through Taiwan from Tokyo, but due to the Taiwan Island Local Officials Conference in late April, and the fact that Taiwan Governor-General Nakagawa had to return to Tokyo on May 2 to discuss important matters with the Japanese government, it was decided to convene it after Nakagawa's return to Taiwan. The Governor-General's authorities had already drafted agreed-upon matters, but now, due to the gradual changes in the situation on the other side, the agenda will be revised again. Furthermore, the Taiwan Governor-General's Police Bureau held a conference of dispatch officers to the other side from April 12th to 14th. In conjunction with the consulate conference on the other side to be convened in June, the Taiwan authorities' emphasis on the situation on the other side is evident. The situation in South China is likely to become tense as a result. (April 25)

Bandit Suppression in Southern Fujian: Yu Sifu Executed; Garrison Announces Yu's Crimes 109

Xiamen Correspondence: Yu Sifu, a notorious bandit from Yongchun and former subordinate of the deceased militia leader Wu Wei, had over a decade of history with bandit militias in Fujian. He wreaked havoc in the areas of Yongchun, Dehua, Datian, Xingquan, and Yongjian, and his standing was comparable to that of Chen Guohui. Yu was recently apprehended in Yongchun by Song Xilian, the commander of the 36th Division and concurrent garrison commander of Quanzhou. His troops were disarmed, and Song ordered his on-the-spot execution to eliminate a scourge of the people. The execution was carried out at approximately 5:00 PM on the 20th of this month by the 106th Brigade Headquarters stationed in Yongchun, in compliance with the order.

Those executed along with Yu were his accomplices Yu Chang, Yu Quan, Chen Derong, and Xu Jie, totaling five individuals. Before the execution, Yu and the others were escorted from the regimental headquarters to the brigade headquarters (the brigade headquarters had relocated from Quanzhou to Yongchun on the 20th). Standing in the courtyard, Brigade Commander Li Liangrong individually inquired about the names of the bandits. Yu immediately said, "I have not done anything wrong. Please, Brigade Commander, investigate thoroughly." Li replied, "I have already investigated and understand clearly. Justice will prevail, and history will prove it." Upon finishing his words, he ordered them to be taken out and executed. Yu Sifu was a native of Funei in Yongchun. He started as a peddler and then entered the greenwoods, where his influence grew daily. In 1928, he served as a brigade commander in the newly organized army, enjoying a period of prominence. He had eight or nine wives and concubines. In August 1929, he was wanted by the provincial government and fled to Datian. His wives, concubines, and servants gradually dispersed. He currently has four wives and concubines. The announcement from the An'nan Yong Border Area Bandit Suppression Command of the 106th Brigade Headquarters is recorded as follows: "Upon investigation, the notorious bandit Yu Sifu and his accomplices Yu Yongchang, Yu Quan, Chen Derong, and Xu Jie have wreaked havoc in the jurisdictions of Yongde and Datian for more than ten years. Numerous complaints have been filed by the people of various counties, piling up like mountains. In 1929, the provincial government issued a reward for their capture. Yu and his gang then fled to Datian. During this campaign against the rebels, Yu again seized the opportunity to come to Yongchun, gathered his followers, occupied the western district, openly engaged in opium and gambling, and extorted money, robbed, and murdered without restraint. We have already detained and disarmed his subordinates. Yu and his gang were also captured on the spot. We have now received an order from Garrison Commander Song to verify the identities of Yu Sifu, Yu Yongchang, Yu Quan, Chen Derong, and Xu Jie and execute them by shooting. In addition to complying with the order, this announcement is made for general knowledge. This announcement." (April 25th)

Fujian Provincial Government Grants Communists Amnesty, Sets Two-Month Deadline to Surrender 110

Fuzhou Correspondence: The 4th Regiment of the Military Police stationed in Fujian uncovered Communist provincial and municipal party headquarters, mutual aid societies, transportation offices, printing presses, the Communist Youth League, and the Anti-Imperialist League in Fuzhou and Xiamen. They arrested more than thirty individuals, including Chen Zhishu, Ni Shigeng, and Guo Bizhen, who held positions such as pseudo-provincial committee secretary, municipal committee secretary, and members. All were granted amnesty to repent and start anew. A special training class was established by the Security Office, and they were sent to study. The course was completed in two months, and they were assigned appropriate jobs. Classes began the day before yesterday. Considering that many Communist members are still in hiding, the provincial government issued an announcement yesterday granting them amnesty if they surrender to the government within two months. The original text is as follows: "According to a report from the 4th Regiment of the Military Police, Chen Zhishu and others, who were recently captured as Communist members, confessed that there are many remaining members who are currently on the run. I propose that Your Excellency publish an announcement in the newspaper granting amnesty to all remaining members who are on the run, in order to save young people who have strayed from the right path and to encourage them to return voluntarily." After investigation, it is found that these remaining members on the run are all weak-willed and have strayed from the right path. While the law cannot tolerate them, their situation is indeed pitiable. If they are allowed to remain in exile, they will inevitably face a dead end with no way to extract themselves. The regiment commander requests that this government publish an announcement granting them amnesty, which should be approved. Therefore, this announcement is hereby made. All remaining members on the run must be aware that they must awaken as soon as possible and resolutely return. Within two months, they must submit a signed pledge of surrender, attach a photo of themselves, and a declaration renouncing communism, and report to this government. Their past actions may then be forgiven, and they will be granted amnesty. They will be educated according to their abilities and procedures, so that they may become useful individuals. If they continue to be deluded and unrepentant after the deadline, they will be wanted by name."

Qi (April 24th)

Northwest Inspection Report: Special Correspondent Geng Ya 111

Observations on the Rise and Fall of Baotou Commerce. Suiyuan, 14th. I went to the train station at 11:00 AM. The train from the east was delayed by about three hours. Mr. Mou Pengling, Bai Xuchu, and others came to see me off. They insisted on returning before the train arrived. The station was flat and filled with people waiting for the train. Many women had bound feet, with red shoes and green trim. The ancient saying "lotus hooks," "three inches," is not an exaggeration. I wanted to step forward and persuade them to liberate themselves first and not inflict this torture on their children, but I felt it was inappropriate in a foreign land, so I hesitated. I saw an old woman leading a group of children, strolling leisurely. One girl in a red jacket, about seven or eight years old, also had bound feet and walked with difficulty, as if in great pain. I asked the old woman, "How can you bear to do this?" She replied, "She (the girl in the red jacket) is a local. I advised her not to bind her feet, but her parents wouldn't allow it. There's nothing I can do. I am from Tanggu. I came here with my husband who works for the railway. I am only fifty years old, but my feet are often cold because they were bound. That's why I don't allow my granddaughters to suffer this living hell." Promoting foot binding release for more than twenty years, and yet seven or eight year old girls have not escaped this misery. No wonder foreigners traveling to the Northwest often take films of men with queues and women with bound feet, labeling them as inferior people. Can those who have a responsibility to guide society continue to turn a blind eye?

The train departed at 4:00 PM. To the north, the Daqing Mountains stood side by side. To the south, the vast expanse of the earth stretched without end. Occasionally, there were deep pits and ditches, with alternating layers of sand and soil, forming symmetrical multi-layered patterns. The ice in the Daqing Mountains had not melted, hanging like white silk. At the Taige Mu, Bikeqi, and Salachi stations, I saw soldiers with disheveled clothes and hats, mixed with many muleteers and laborers. I knew they were soldiers from Sun Dianying's disbanded army. When the train stopped before reaching the station platform, women with bound feet found it very difficult to get off. Railway police helped them down, and they hurried away, not daring to look up. Outside the station, coachmen competed to greet passengers. They rode skillfully, but walked unsteadily. The people of the north are strong and good riders, and even women are no exception. If they did not bind their feet, wouldn't it further enhance their health and beauty?

The road gradually approached the Hetao region. The fields on both sides, with mountain springs to the north and canals to the south, were incomparably fertile. Where there were villages, there were also many trees. The fields were connected by footpaths, and the ditches crisscrossed. Farmers drove oxen to plow the fields, engaging in spring plowing. Further from the villages, the ground was fish-scale-like, covered with weeds and overgrown with vegetation, as if it had been cultivated and then abandoned. The train traveled for dozens of miles, and the view remained vast and endless. It is a pity to abandon the land.

I arrived in Baotou at 10:00 PM. Two or three miles into the city, young men carried luggage on their backs, using hemp ropes tightly pressed against their shoulders. It was clear that they were not strong enough, and carrying the luggage was unnatural. However, they were afraid that their business would be taken by others, so they struggled to move forward. Before they had gone a few hundred steps, sweat was pouring down their faces in the cold weather. If they could change from carrying to using a carrying pole, it might reduce their labor. The city gate was closed, but opened again when we called. Several guards did not inspect us. The streets were narrow, uneven, and unkempt. Dust flew in our faces, and the electric lights were dim. I stayed at the Taian Inn. The room next door was occupied by a demobilization office of a certain unit. Demobilized officers, their families stranded here, were forced by circumstances to wait to return east and came to collect their demobilization pay so they could leave tomorrow. However, the office was waiting for verification and was not willing to issue the payments immediately, causing a disturbance that lasted until dawn.

The earthen city of Baotou was built in the Tongzhi era and was nineteen miles in circumference. It was originally a town in Salachi County. In 1923, a governance bureau was established, and in 1926, it was changed to a county. It is located eight miles north of the Yellow River, at the end of the PingSui Railway, with convenient water and land transportation. Goods from Tianjin, Shaanxi, Gansu, Inner and Outer Mongolia all gathered and dispersed here. It is extremely important militarily and commercially. In the spring of 1933, a preparatory office for the municipal government was established. However, due to the lack of a comprehensive plan for the new municipal government's finances, it has not yet been established. The total area of the county is 47,400 square miles, with a population of over 17,300 households, totaling about 70,000 people. About 20,000 to 30,000 people live in the city. At the beginning of the establishment of the county, the business of various merchants was thriving, showing a trend of rapid progress. However, later, due to (1) the independence of Outer Mongolia, (2) the blockage of the western route, (3) the depreciation of Jin currency, and (4) the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, business suffered a huge blow, and business plummeted. Bankruptcies and closures were heard of daily. The rise and fall of various businesses in Baotou is specially inquired about from the Chamber of Commerce and listed as follows:

Business Type Peak Period Number of Businesses Total Capital (10,000 Yuan)

Money Exchange 1926 15 25

Spring 1937 13 7.2

Fur & Leather 1925 28 12.5

Spring 1937 14 5.5

General Goods 1926 140 35

Spring 1937 99 25

Wholesale Stores 1926 15 5

Spring 1937 8 2.5

Mongolian Goods Before Outer Mongolia 500 Unknown

Lost

After Outer Mongolia 11 4

Lost

Rice & Flour 1926 120 Unknown

Oil & Grain 1926 23 Unknown

Spring 1937 8 6.5

Livestock Unknown Unknown Unknown

Spring 1937 7 0.5

Cloth Business 1926 75 Unknown

Spring 1937 22 6.5

Transportation 1929 17 2.5

Spring 1937 10 1.1

(Note) "Wholesale Stores" refers to wholesale dealers; "Mongolian Goods" refers to businesses specializing in trade with Mongolians.

Since the independence of Outer Mongolia, the Mongolian goods business has declined from 500 businesses to only 11. Currently, in addition to doing business with Inner Mongolia, they are also secretly trading with Outer Mongolians, which is called "stealing," but the profits are limited, and there is always the risk of being caught and confiscated. Therefore, although there are many reasons for the decline of Baotou's commerce, the severance of relations with Outer Mongolia is indeed the biggest fatal blow. This is not only the case in Baotou, but also in the ports along the PingSui Line, such as Zhangjiakou and GuiSui. However, Baotou has the advantage of being the hub of water and land transportation in the Northwest, and it is also the source of development in the Northwest. At this time of developing the Northwest and starting construction, all needs must rely on Baotou for supply, and future production will also rely on Baotou for export. The future holds great promise, and it is not only easy to restore the prosperity of a few years ago, but it can even reach the prosperity of Tianjin, Shanghai, and Wuhan. If the local officials and merchants can unite and work together towards the goal of construction, then success will be within reach. (18th)

Jiangxi Province: Guangchang Imminent; Bandit Suppression Army Very Close to Guangchang County; Bandit Stronghold on the Border of Xinfeng About to Be Captured 112

Nanchang Correspondence: The bandit suppression in Jiangxi Province has been achieving victories recently. The recovery of bandit areas, the construction of roads, the construction of blockhouses, the reception of refugees, and the organization of the people have all been completed. Recently, our army has advanced towards the bandit stronghold in Guangchang, consolidating and building as it advances. Since the offensive, we have captured dangerous passes one after another. Yesterday, Division Commander Xiao Zhiping telegraphed that his division captured Yunji Village and Guanfu Ridge on the 22nd, defeating the pseudo-35th Army Corps, seizing more than 200 guns. The bandits' fighting power has been lost, and they are fleeing at the sight of our troops. Our vanguard is only ten miles away from Guangchang City. Our army will advance again after clearing and recovering the remaining bandits in various places. Guangchang City will be captured soon. In addition, Nanfeng County Chief Liao Guoping recently telegraphed the provincial government, saying that our army has advanced to Shazi Ridge, and Guangchang County is within sight. From now on, cooperation in suppression and post-war reconstruction is eagerly awaited. The military authorities are entrusting Nanfeng to handle all matters related to bandit suppression in the territory of Guangchang, but due to the distance and complexity of the matters, it is feared that there may be delays, which may delay military opportunities. It is proposed that the newly appointed Guangchang County Magistrate Liu be ordered to take over as soon as possible to facilitate the advancement of the suppression.

Fengcheng News: Beishan, on the border of Xinfeng, was originally a stronghold of the Red Bandits. Since the large-scale encirclement and suppression by the five counties last year, the bandits have scattered. However, due to the dangerous mountain roads, the army adopted a steady approach and did not conduct a thorough search. However, the bandits hiding in the mountains did not dare to move. Recently, due to the shortage of supplies, the bandits sent people down the mountain to purchase food. The people reported this to the 3rd Security Regiment stationed there, which surrounded the area at dawn on the 19th. The officers and soldiers bravely advanced, and the remaining bandits had no resistance. More than 100 people were captured on the spot, and more than 30 rifles and countless other bandit supplies were seized. The bandits looked emaciated.

Their hardship can be imagined. After this bandit den is broken, it can be said to be the removal of a hidden danger for Xinfeng and other counties.

Le'an News: Our army is actively engaged in the construction of motor roads in the recovered bandit areas to facilitate transportation. It is learned that the 27th Division stationed in Le'an is particularly diligent in road construction. Previously, the road from Le'an to Lugang was reinforced with gravel, so that automobiles can travel smoothly without hindrance, even in rainy weather. More than 10,000 saplings have been planted along the road, and all are now in full bloom with green leaves. Recently, in order to expand the bandit area, the 79th Brigade and directly subordinate units have been sent to build the motor road from Le'an to Zengtian. Although there have been heavy rains recently, the officers and soldiers are still working hard to build the road as usual. The project is expected to be completed within a few days. (April 26th)

Some Rickshaw Pullers Have Resumed Work 115

The general strike of rickshaw pullers in Suzhou has lasted for three days. After the party and government organs decided on a solution and strictly investigated the instigators, Shen Weiyang, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, saw that some rickshaw pullers had resumed work on the afternoon of the 27th, but were still being blocked. He went to Huaiyang Road outside the Shantangmen Gate at 6:00 AM on the 28th, accompanied by an inspector from the Third Branch Bureau, to persuade the rickshaw pullers who lived there to resume work. Most of them complied and resumed work. However, some striking rickshaw pullers went around blocking, beating the working rickshaw pullers. At the same time, they also coerced the horse-drawn carriage drivers to join the strike. When the horse-drawn carriage drivers refused, their carriages were destroyed. Chief Shen immediately led the police to arrest Ni Hesong and Jiang Erwangzi, the leaders, outside the Xu Gate, and Chen Xuejin, a rickshaw puller in western attire, on Huaiyang Road, who was suspected of inciting the strike. They were immediately sent to the headquarters for strict interrogation. The Public Security Bureau has decided to take strict measures against rickshaw pullers who prevent others from resuming work. However, yesterday, about 1,000 rickshaw pullers resumed work in the city.

Station Master Released Opium Smuggler, Ordered to Be Sent to Nanchang 116

After Station Master Zhuang of Suzhou Station was reported by the railway police for releasing a major criminal who smuggled raw materials for opium pills, the Railway Administration detained Station Master Zhuang and sent officials to investigate and verify the facts. Changshu: The Rent Collection Office Is Closed 117

Last winter, the farmers in various villages owed a large amount of rent to various landlords, so the landlords specially requested the county to strictly pursue the rent. The county government then established a rent collection office at this time, appointing Xu Chunian as the director, specializing in handling the rent affairs between landlords and tenants, resulting in all farmers who were unable to pay the rent being detained. As a result, there were three to four hundred people detained in the detention center. Now that the busy farming season has arrived, and the spring harvest is about to begin, the county government, in order not to harm agricultural affairs, closed the rent collection office. However, the farmers who are still in detention have not yet completed their payment, so on the afternoon of the 27th, Director Xu gathered the rent collectors to the county to announce the following two points: (1) The public servants are required to bail out the detained tenants within one week. (2) The public servants are responsible for paying the tenants' outstanding meal expenses in detention. However, the public servants seemed reluctant. Finally, they expressed the opinion that it would be impossible for them to be responsible for the meal expenses and that they should be collected from the local servants. Director Xu agreed to consider this.

Wuxi: The Replacement for the Chief of the Public Security Bureau Has Been Found 118

Li Wengong, the chief of the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, resigned and went to Shanghai after the Gu Li Shuyun case and the resignation of Gu Renfa, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs. All duties were temporarily performed by Chief Inspector Zhang Yu. The provincial government meeting has now approved the appointment of Chen Yuchu to fill the vacancy. Chen is from Hangzhou County, Zhejiang Province, and has served as the director of the Nanjing Municipal Police Department and the chief of the Accounting Section of the Bureau of Finance. He recently came south from Peiping and arrived in Zhenjiang the day before yesterday. After being appointed, he will make arrangements and come to Wuxi to take up his new post at the beginning of the month.

Provincial Governor: Active Improvement of Toll Calls 119

Since the Department of Construction has actively developed toll calls in Jiangsu Province, there has been special progress. In the past year, the original twelve counties including Nanjing have been expanded to the counties north of the Yangtze River, making transportation between the north and south of the Yangtze River increasingly convenient. Recently, Director Shen of the Department of Construction found that the old regulations for provincial long-distance calls in various counties were no longer applicable, so he drafted new regulations and distributed them to the counties, which will be implemented from May 5th. Fees will be charged according to the new regulations in the future. There have also been many improvements in other areas. The calls are divided into six types: official calls, ordinary calls, urgent calls, scheduled calls, news calls, and special official calls. In addition, there have been many changes in the application methods and transmission methods. New regulations have been formulated for the upper fees. The prices for ordinary calls have been revised as follows: From Wuxi to Jiangyin, Wu County, and Wujin, 30 cents; Changshu and Yixing, 40 cents; Liyang, Danyang, and Jintan, 60 cents; Jurong and Lishui, 80 cents; Zhenjiang, 65 cents; Nanjing, 95 cents. The fees for delivering telephone calls are particularly low. The Wuxi township telephone areas that are connected to long-distance calls include Tangqiao, Nanfangquan, Daqiangmen, Houzhai, Dangkou, Zhangshe, Xinqiao, Anzhen, Houqiao, Yanjiaqiao, Zhajiaqiao, Xingtang, Zhangjingqiao, Zhaimen, Donghudang, Huangtutang, Chenshu, Wangzhuang, Yangjian, Huai, Yangyuan, and Xueyanqiao, a total of twenty-two towns.

Cold Weather Delays Sericulture 120

Since last month, the weather in the county has been cold, and residents have had to wear cotton clothes. The cold weather has been even worse in recent days. Yesterday (the 28th), it rained, and the temperature dropped to 63 degrees. In previous years, people had to wear single clothes on this day. Therefore, the sprouting of mulberry leaves in the countryside has been very slow. They are now only the size of copper coins. There is a saying in the county that "silk worms will have white heads three days after Grain Rain." Grain Rain has now passed for a week, but the silk worms have not yet begun to spin cocoons. If the weather remains cold, they will still not be able to spin cocoons in the coming days. Therefore, the silkworm farming in this season has been delayed by ten days.

Jiangyin: Fortress Commander Asks the County to Borrow Money 121

Xie Muhan, the commander of the Jiangyin Fortress, asked County Magistrate Bao to raise 5,000 yuan because the Ministry of Military Affairs had not paid its expenses and supplies were difficult to obtain. After Bao approved the letter, he sent letters to local gentry, merchants, farmers, the Bank of China, etc. at 2:00 PM on the 27th to discuss the distribution method at a meeting in the county government.

Three Years of Illegal Items Will Be Burned on Schedule 122

From the time of the former county magistrate Li Leng to the present, all the gambling tools and narcotic drugs confiscated by law, as well as the certificates, that have been confiscated for three years by the end of March will be publicly burned on May 8th with the approval of the people's hall and the high court, and officials will be invited to supervise the burning.

Zhencheng Road to Open to Traffic in June 123

The Zhencheng Road project is vast and has taken two years to complete. The roadbed is now gradually being completed in various sections. However, the soil is very loose and cannot be covered with gravel immediately, so vehicles must travel over it for several months, and it must sink at least five inches below the new construction level before it can be stable. Therefore, after the road is completed, trial runs must be conducted at the end of May, and gravel must be paved again in mid-July. The full road opening ceremony must be held on June 15th, when the Seven-Province Transportation Exhibition opens, and will be held in Zhenjiang by Committee Chairman Jiang and others.

Zhenjiang: Provincial Land Bureau Investigates Property Rights in British Concession 124

Regarding the regulations on foreign churches renting land in the interior and issuing permanent lease licenses, the provincial land bureau had previously ordered the Zhenjiang County Land Bureau to follow them. However, the foreign properties in the former British concession in Zhenjiang should be registered and licensed by the county land bureau for inventory purposes after the Qing Dynasty. However, before handling this, it must be clarified whether permanent lease contracts were exchanged in accordance with the Sino-British exchange of notes when the concession was recovered in 1919, how many households there are, and whether the permanent leases have expired. All of these should be investigated separately for reference. Yesterday, the county land bureau was ordered to investigate and report the above-mentioned items separately as soon as possible.

Recent Developments in Two Construction Projects 125

The Shayao River in Zhenjiang has been actively underway since it started construction. According to the report from Director Lin of the Engineering Office, the project is divided into three sections, and the middle and north sections will be completed by the end of the month. The south section will be completed later, but it will also be completed in a few days. After that, more than 80,000 mu of farmland in the area will be able to enjoy water conservancy and obtain more harvests. The Zhencheng Road has been expedited since it was ordered to be built. The fourth district has already been contracted to build the road, and it can be completed by the end of the month. The section of the first district near the city will be contracted out, and it is estimated that more than 12,000 yuan will be needed. Director Shen has agreed to allocate 8,000 yuan, and another 4,000 yuan will be raised from the county construction funds. Construction will begin soon. However, the first district is the most difficult because 20 to 30 ponds need to be filled, which will have a great impact on the irrigation of farmers. If the soil is excavated from the farmland next to the ponds, the losses of the people will be even more unbearable. It has now been decided to avoid excavating soil from the farmland next to the ponds, and if it is absolutely necessary, only inferior fields will be excavated, and a request will be submitted to exempt the Jeng rice and issue land prices to reduce the losses of the people.

Nantong: Deadline to Eradicate All Narcotics in the County 126

The Magistrate of Nantong County, Cheng, with the implementation of the Baojia system at this time, has strictly implemented the eradication of narcotics. It has been decided that on May 1st, all the teams and bureaus in the county will mobilize to carry out inspections, and within ten days, they will thoroughly investigate the manufacturing agencies, opium dens, and the manufacturers, transporters, and sellers of narcotics and opium, and close and arrest them separately.

Renowned Bandit in Dongxiang Captured 127

Zhang Kui, a renowned bandit in Dongxiang, has committed many crimes and has not been captured for a long time. The bandit recently sneaked back, and the prosecutor's office of the court sent police to arrest him. After interrogation, he was sent to prison.

Jiashan: Two Cases of Suicide 128

(1) Tang Xiaodi, a resident of Qianyao Town in the county, married Liang, and they had children. The family was poor. Two years ago, he borrowed 100 yuan from his wife's younger sister. Over the years, his wife's younger sister repeatedly demanded the debt from her brother-in-law, so Xiaodi beat her severely. Fortunately, others persuaded them, and she was rescued. Unexpectedly, Xiaodi went home and insulted his wife Liang. Liang was filled with resentment and jumped into the river last night and committed suicide. (2) Xu Jiesan, a resident of Luxu Town, married Jiang Zheng and had only one daughter, Aibao, who had just reached the age of fifteen. This spring, a relative acted as a matchmaker and betrothed her to someone with the surname Xi in Xitang. Jiang negotiated and agreed, but Jiesan did not agree. Later, when Jiesan found out, he was very displeased and scolded Jiang, causing Jiang to become angry and inconsolable. She committed suicide by hanging herself behind people's backs. When she was discovered, she was already dead.

Hangzhou Continued Hearing of the Wang Hanlun Case 129

Wang Hanlun (i.e., Peng Jianqing) sued Wang Jihuan for divorce. The Hangzhou County Local Court held a continued hearing yesterday (the 28th) at 9:30 AM, presided over by Yang Delin, a judge from the Civil Division, accompanied by female clerk Tong Wenbao. The courtroom was crowded with onlookers, including over thirty students from a certain girls' school. The judge questioned Wang Jihuan about her age and origin, followed by Wang Hanlun. Hanlun eloquently recounted Jihuan's mistreatment and the circumstances of her leaving home. He stated that a delayed divorce was also acceptable, and requested an investigation into who was deceiving whom. Wang Jihuan was then questioned, and she denied the mistreatment. Finally, the maid, Wen Ma, was questioned. The judge instructed both parties to go outside and attempt a reconciliation. Jihuan claimed she could not afford to rent another house. At 11:30 AM, the court adjourned.

Strange Warship Opens Fire in Changshu; Navy Has Not Received Report; Jiankang Warship Docked in Nantong Will Surely Clarify in the Future 138

According to the Guowen News Agency, two strange warships fired two live rounds while passing Gao Pu Kou in Changshu. The shells landed in farmland. At the same time, residents along the river heard machine gun fire, which lasted for half an hour. Yesterday, the reporter inquired with both the Chinese and Japanese sides in Mupu. According to the Japanese consulate, the naval landing party has not received any news of warships firing artillery near Changshu. The Chinese navy stated that there must be a prior notification for any foreign ships to conduct live fire tests along the river. They also stated that they have not received confirmation of the foreign ship firing in Changshu. The nationality of the warship is even more unclear. The reporter further inquired about the situation of Laoshusha and the stationing of Chinese warships along the river. It was said that there were many floating markers along the Changshu riverfront, and the river surface was very narrow. The beaches, such as Laoshusha Baimaosha, are numerous. Although the Jiankang warship is currently docked in Nantong, the Langshan mountain screens the view from the Nantong riverfront directly to the Changshu riverfront, and even the sound of artillery fire cannot be transmitted. Therefore, before it can be proven whether this event occurred, it will surely be clarified in the future. As Nantong is the throat of the Yangtze River, any foreign ships entering or leaving will be clearly visible and easy to identify. The inscriptions on the shells will provide a general indication. As for piracy, the area from Nantong to the Changshu riverfront has traditionally been peaceful because there are many beaches and few islands, leaving pirates with nowhere to hide. Moreover, it would be sufficient to deal with bandits with machine guns. There is no need to use artillery bombardment.

International Problems Research Association's Opinion on Japan's Statement: Absurd and Unreasonable, Attempting to Monopolize China, No Foreigners Allowed to Usurp Rights in Establishing National Defense 139

Since the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued an informal statement on Sino-Japanese relations on the 17th of this month, it has caused a great international reaction. Our government has also issued two statements refuting it. Recently, the International Problems Research Association issued the following opinion on Japan's statement:

Wanting to Monopolize ChinaOn the 17th of this month, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued a statement on China, seemingly acting as the sole protector of East Asia and treating our country as if it were its vassal state. All matters of international cooperation with us, even those of a technical nature without any political implications, are being opposed. Japan's statement believes that "After the Manchurian and Shanghai incidents, any joint action taken by foreign countries, even in the name of technical or financial assistance, naturally contains political implications..."

"In principle, we must oppose such undertakings." Today, Japan stubbornly insists that "technical or financial cooperation naturally contains political implications." Regardless of whether such a statement has the suspicion of overstepping boundaries and interfering in the internal affairs of neighboring countries, its overbearing attitude is filled with political implications. Japan is using the excuse of not wanting the great powers to jointly manage China in order to monopolize and annex China.

Unlimited AmbitionPreviously, Japan only shamelessly claimed that the three northeastern provinces were its special sphere of influence. Since the "September 18th" incident, relying on its aggressive and brutal means, it has seized our Northeast and is now insatiably seeking to dominate East Asia and fulfill its Monroe Doctrine in East Asia. Today's statement declares its desire to "fulfill its special responsibilities in East Asia." Tomorrow, why can't it go further and wildly claim to fulfill its responsibilities in the Pacific, or even the world?

Exceeding the Twenty-One DemandsThe current statement by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs represents the ambitions of its militarism. At the beginning of the European War, the European and American powers had no time to look east. Japan believed that a good opportunity was rare and thus presented us with the Twenty-One Demands. Today's crisis in the international situation is indeed like the eve of the outbreak of the European War, and the content of Japan's current statement is a reiteration of the spirit of the demands made in the fourth year of the Republic. The most alarming of the Twenty-One Demands was the "Fifth Item," which aimed to take over China's military and national defense. Today's statement says, "As for supplying China with military aircraft, building airfields in China, dispatching military training officers or military advisors to China, or raising loans to supply funds for political purposes, it is clearly possible...to disrupt the peace and order of East Asia. Japan will oppose such actions." These words are not only consistent, but also exceed the rigid demands of the Twenty-One Demands. Then, Japan advocated taking over China's military and national defense. Now, it forces the great powers not to cooperate with China. While its words are divided into passive and active, its purpose is the same.

Absurd and ContradictoryNational defense construction is a right that an independent country should have, and no other country can interfere. The Japanese army can occupy neighboring countries' land and prepare for offensive and aggressive military actions, while China alone cannot consciously engage in defensive and self-defense national defense construction on its own territory. Cuckoos occupy magpie nests, and guests usurp the role of the host. Can any nation with blood not bristle with anger? Japan's statement also says, "Japan earnestly desires the unification of China, the preservation of China's territorial integrity, and the restoration of order within China." It is perplexing to read this. Has Japan forgotten that it used force to destroy China's territorial integrity not long ago, seizing our four northeastern provinces and occupying them to this day?

Iwai, Representative of the Japanese Embassy's Information Bureau, Issues a Statement: Completely Fallacious and Dogmatic, Attempting to Cover Up 140

According to the Dagong News Agency, since Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota issued an informal statement opposing the League of Nations' technical cooperation with China, all countries in the world have condemned Japan's actions as arrogant and will unite to deal with Japan. They also pointed out that Japan's actions not only violate the Nine-Power Treaty but also disrupt world peace. In light of the increasingly deteriorating international sentiment, Iwai Eiichi, the representative of the Japanese Embassy's Information Bureau, issued a statement, resorting to sophistry and trying to confuse the world's hearing. Here is a record of it:

Opposing the League of Nations' Investment in China 141

According to Iwai Eiichi, if the League of Nations invests in China with a pure attitude while upholding the principles of equal opportunity and open doors, Japan will naturally sympathize with it. However, the current investment of the League of Nations in China is actually being diverted to military and political purposes. This move will actually promote internal strife in China. Japan has the responsibility to maintain peace in East Asia and must oppose it.

Declaring the Intent of the Hirota Declaration 142

As for Japan's intention, it is to hope that China can achieve the goal of peaceful unification in order to achieve coexistence and co-prosperity between China and Japan. However, China's attitude is the opposite. Therefore, Foreign Minister Hirota specifically issued an informal statement to warn the League of Nations. Unfortunately, some points in the statement were not noted, causing misunderstandings in various countries. Therefore, he is issuing another statement today to explain.

Accusing China of Having an Inappropriate Attitude 143

Kishii continued to translate, saying that China actually took this opportunity to abandon its past pro-Japanese rhetoric, incite anti-Japanese sentiment, and instigate countries around the world to oppose Japan. At the same time, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs instructed the ambassadors to the United States and the United Kingdom to contact the United States and the United Kingdom separately to promote full cooperation between the United States and the United Kingdom, and to convene a meeting of the nine signatory countries in England or the United States on May 15 to pressure Japan. This move is extremely inappropriate.

Using Pretexts to Frighten the Chinese Government 144

The Chinese government remains calm on the surface at this juncture to avoid arousing public resentment and provoking Japan's anger. However, the Chinese government still does not abandon its policy of "using barbarians to control barbarians" to undermine peace in East Asia. If any problems arise in the future, this responsibility should be borne by China.

Denying Rumors of Personnel Changes at the Japanese Embassy 145

Iwai also said that rumors of changes in the Japanese Ambassador to China after his return home to report on Sino-Japanese issues to Foreign Minister Hirota are not true. Reports that Consul General Suma, stationed in Nanjing, came to Shanghai from Nanjing on the order of Foreign Minister Hirota to explain Japan's statement to the consuls of various countries in Shanghai to avoid misunderstandings are also not true. Suma has always been in Nanjing and has not set foot in Shanghai.

中航機昨停飛　因天氣惡劣故 155

China Aviation Corporation Flights Suspended Yesterday Due to Bad Weather

It is reported by the China East News Agency that the China Aviation Corporation's airmail flights on various routes were unable to depart on schedule the day before yesterday due to the influence of heavy fog and bad weather. 法華區地稅　定下月十六正式開徵

French Concession Land Tax Scheduled to be Officially Levied on the 16th of Next Month

財政局佈告法華區開征日期

Finance Bureau Announces Date for Levying Tax in the French Concession

蒲淞區地價日内可估價完竣

Land Prices in the Puxi-Songjiang Area Expected to be Assessed Completely Within Days

Following the successful implementation of the land value tax in the Shanghai South and Zhabei districts, the land value assessment in the French Concession has also been completed. According to an announcement by the Finance Bureau, the official levy will begin on May 16th. The assessment in the Puxi-Songjiang area is also largely completed and is expected to be levied within days. Details are as follows:

財政局佈告

Finance Bureau Announcement

The Finance Bureau issued an announcement yesterday regarding the levy of land value tax, stating, "Regarding the levy of land value tax in the first, second, third, and fourth districts of the French Concession, according to the 'Provisional Regulations for the Levy of Land Value Tax' and the scope and start date of the levy, which have been announced and implemented by the Municipal Government, the land within the Tian, Di, Yuan, Huang, Yu, Zhou, Hong, Ri, Yue, Ying, and Ze blocks of the first, second, third, and fourth districts of the French Concession has been assessed by the Land Valuation Committee and submitted to the Land Bureau and this Bureau for approval and announcement by the Municipal Government. All land within the assessed area should pay the second installment of the land value tax for the 22nd year of the Republic, at a rate of 5/6ths. The levy will commence on May 16th of this year and must be completed within two months, ending on July 15th of this year. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be subject to case referral and collection in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for the Levy of Land Value Tax and Article 23 of the Implementing Rules, including the imposition of annual interest on the outstanding amount and the extraction of income from the land or sale of the land for debt repayment, as stipulated. In addition to sending separate notices, this announcement is issued for all taxpayers to comply with and pay at the Municipal West Collection Office at the intersection of Route de Robert and Avenue de la Bigne within the deadline. Failure to do so will result in penalties. Those who have not received their notices should, within the deadline, provide the location of the land, block number, and current address or mailing address to the Bureau for verification and supplementary issuance of a copy. Do not delay or neglect. This is specially announced." Director Cai Zengji.

張素民講統制經濟

Zhang Sumin Lectures on Controlled Economy

The other day, Daxia University specially invited economic expert Dr. Zhang Sumin to lecture on "What is Controlled Economy". Hundreds of people attended the lecture. After the lecture, the whole hall applauded. It has been found out that Dr. Zhang's lecture is as follows: Controlled economy has two meanings, broad and narrow. The broad sense of controlled economy is government intervention policy. Interference policy, on the surface, is familiar to us, but in Europe and the United States, it has only been around for seven or eight years. Before the middle of the 19th century, the economy of Europe and the United States was entirely dominated by liberalism. After the middle of the 19th century, economic relations became more complicated, and the conflicts between social classes became more intense, so the governments of various countries had to adopt intervention policies. The narrow sense of controlled economy is a further step, that is, the government's planned and systematic intervention in the economic activities of the people, so that they are connected, balanced and developed. Its essential elements are planning and connection, so it is also called economic planning or planned economy. However, this kind of control is easier to carry out in countries where the means of production are publicly owned, and slightly more difficult in countries where property is privately owned. In recent years, the call for controlled economy has been high because countries are seeking a way out of economic panic. In terms of what has been done in various countries, it can be divided into three systems: (1) the British and American system or the democratic system, (2) the Italian and German system or the Fascist system, and (3) the Soviet Russian system or the socialist system. The degree of implementation in the United Kingdom is not as good as in the United States, Germany is not as good as in Italy, and Soviet Russia is a completely planned economy. The fifth five-year plan has been completed, and it is now the second year of its second five-year plan. The Economic Commission of China should pay attention to planning in the future, and control without planning is difficult to achieve results.

外貨傾銷中　我國電業界近况

Foreign Goods Dumped: Recent Situation of China's Electrical Industry

外國燈泡在滬製造

Foreign Light Bulbs Manufactured in Shanghai

China's electrical manufacturing industry has been progressing rapidly in recent years, which has attracted great attention from foreign merchants, who have repeatedly devised various methods to defeat Chinese factories. After the January 28th Incident, a foreign merchant's famous flashlight factory came to China to set up a factory to manufacture flashlights and dumped them at low prices. As a result, the foreign merchant's factory failed and closed down due to the low overhead of Chinese factories. At the same time, inferior small light bulbs were dumped in China, but the association managed to resist them, so they could not compete and stopped. Recently, foreign light bulb merchants, because of the progress of Chinese-made light bulbs, were panicked. As of the spring of last year, they organized a foreign light bulb company and tried their best to attack Chinese light bulb factories. For a year, because most Chinese people gradually became patriotic, no effect was seen. Recently, seeing that their plan failed, they released a sub-brand and sold it at a discounted price. However, most users in various places already know that the so-called foreign light bulbs are also manufactured in Shanghai, but are divided into several foreign trademarks. 雄鷄牌毛巾商標勝利　行政院認局部核駁均爲不合

Xiongji Brand Towel Trademark Victory: The Executive Yuan Believes That Partial Rejection is Inappropriate

雄雞牌成立雞球牌不准註册

Xiongji Brand Established, Jiqiu Brand Not Allowed to Register

Mr. Ling Pengfei, manager of Jinglun Cotton Weaving Factory, for the Jiqu Brand trademark of Huaxing Towel Factory, after re-appealing to the Executive Yuan, the Executive Yuan decided that Jinglun had the final victory. The decision of the Executive Yuan is recorded below: (Twenty-third Year Litigation No. 9) Re-Appellant, Ling Pengfei, manager of Jinglun Cotton Weaving Factory, male, 56 years old, from Nanhui, residing at Yuchangxiang Towel Shop, No. 8 Dongjiadu, Shanghai. The right re-appellant filed a re-appeal to this court due to disagreement with the decision of the Ministry of Industry in a trademark dispute case with Huaxing Towel Factory. The decision of this court is as follows: (Main text) The original disposition and decision are both revoked. The Jiqu Brand trademark of Huaxing Towel Factory in this case should not be allowed to register. (Facts) The re-appellant submitted to the Trademark Bureau the Jiqu Brand trademark No. 13939 of Huaxing Towel Factory for use on towel products, believing that it was similar to the Xiongji Brand trademark No. 42 and the Diqiu Brand trademark No. 12916 that the re-appellant used on the same product and were already registered, and had a suspicion of imitation. He repeatedly raised objections to the Trademark Bureau, but they were all rejected. The re-appellant did not agree with this disposition and appealed to the Ministry of Industry, but was rejected again. Still not satisfied, he filed a re-appeal to the court. (Reasons) If the text and graphics of two or more trademarks objectively have the risk of causing confusion among buyers, they are similar. In this case, the Jiqu Brand trademark of Huaxing Towel Factory approved by the Trademark Bureau uses the chicken and the ball as the graphic pattern of the trademark. Comparing it with the Xiongji Brand trademark and the Diqiu Brand trademark registered by the re-appellant, the words "chicken" and "ball" are the same in the text, and the graphics all use the chicken or the ball as the main part of the trademark. Although the colors used by the two parties are different, the chickens have differences in whether their beaks are open or their tails are raised, and the patterns of the balls are also different, it is inevitable that there will be confusion among buyers at different times and places. The Trademark Bureau and the Ministry of Industry's request for the re-appellant regarding the Jiqu Brand trademark of Huaxing Towel Factory not to be allowed to register is unavoidable and inappropriate. Based on the above conclusions, this re-appeal is justified. Therefore, in accordance with the previous paragraph of Article 9 of the litigation law, the main text is decided, March 24th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, President Wang Zhaoming.

Various Groups Will Rise Up to Help

Pederi on Xinzha Road has been without water for five days because the Catholic Church, the landlord, demanded an increase in water fees, and ordered the water company to install meters for each household, which was rejected by the tenants. The landlord cut off the water supply on the 24th. The landlord has shown no remorse, although a public tap has been opened on Xinzha Road, thousands of tenants are scrambling for water, which is not enough, and it is extremely crowded.

租用水缸　All the tenants have implemented emergency relief measures, rented more than 100 water tanks from a certain tank store, distributed one to each household, hired two porters, and prepared to resist for a long time. It will not stop until the goal of unconditionally restoring the water supply is achieved.

赴工部局　Tenants' representatives have repeatedly negotiated with the Municipal Council through their lawyers, but there has been no concrete response. Yesterday, Zhang Zhizeng, a representative of the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee, went to the Municipal Council for serious negotiations and demanded a quick solution.

裝表斷水　There is a tiger stove and a Tangsongji glass car edge workshop in Pederi. Because of the nature of their business, they are all equipped with water meters. This time, they were also cut off from water. It is even more

Sports News: Guanghua and Central Divide the Spoils; Jiangnan University Athletics Championship: Guanghua Retains Track Title, Central Wins Field Title Again; Central Sweeps Women's Titles; Twelve New Jiangnan University Records Set by Men and Women

The Jiangnan University 7th Annual Athletics Meet, held at Zhenru and Jinan University over the past two days, concluded yesterday. Guanghua University retained the track championship, while Central University secured the field championship. The women's championship was again swept by Central. The weather was uncooperative, greatly diminishing the enjoyment, and thus the results were mediocre. However, while far from our ideal expectations, progress was indeed made. Men broke seven Jiangnan University records, women broke four, and one new event record was set, totaling five. This is also somewhat satisfactory. Score table for each school: Guanghua and Central Universities continue to dominate the "track" and "field" respectively, each retaining their championship for another year. Guanghua's track success was due to the Dong brothers and Tao Yingjie, who secured six first-place finishes. Only the 10,000 meters and high hurdles fell into other hands. Central also captured five first-place finishes in field events, only missing out on high jump and long jump. Women's athletics was entirely Central's domain. The scores are listed below:

Today's Athletics Match: Far East Games Athletes vs. Shanghai Westerners at 2 PM at the China Athletics Field: A Gathering of Talents, a Spectacle to Behold

To prepare our country's athletics team for the Far East Games, a friendly match has been arranged against a Shanghai Westerners team at 2 PM today at the China Athletics Field on Father Laoshen Road. This gathering of national elites against outstanding athletes from various countries in Shanghai provides an opportunity to hone skills, and exceptional results are expected. The participating teams include 27 athletes from our side (the Western team list is not yet finalized). Number bibs for all athletes can be collected from the Association for the Advancement of Physical Culture at 10 AM today. Order at the venue will be maintained by the East Asia Physical Education College Boy Scouts. Admission tickets are uniformly priced at six dimes, and entry will be through the Sapor Road entrance. This competition is purely for practice and will not be scored. Participating athletes' events will be decided on the spot, so pre-grouping is not possible. Far East Games: Japanese Athletes Departed Yesterday; A Delegation of 163 Members

(United Japanese News Agency, Kobe, 28th) Regardless of whether it's for or against participation in the Far East Games, public opinion is divided. However, the delegation of athletes has decided to embark on their expedition amidst this swirl of opinion. At 10 AM on the 28th, amidst a heavy police presence and strict security measures, the delegation of 166 members boarded six buses. They boarded the special ship "Taihe Maru" at noon, and it is scheduled to set sail at 3 PM on the 29th. It is reported that the athletes are waiting quietly in their cabins before departure.

Breakdown of Athletes and Staff (United Japanese News Agency, Kobe, 28th): The breakdown of the athlete delegation on the "Taihe Maru" is as follows:

Nambu Unable to Attend Due to Foot Injury (United Japanese News Agency, Osaka, 28th): Chūhei Nambu, considered a world-class athlete in jumping, suddenly announced before departure that his foot pain had not fully recovered and requested to withdraw from the Far East Games. It is said that his inability to attend is entirely due to his foot injury and has nothing to do with the issue of non-participation.

(Electric News Agency, Tokyo, 28th): At 11:30 PM last night, five thugs, each armed with a five-foot-long bamboo spear, attempted to break into the Athlete's Hotel, the lodging for the athletes from the Asia Rink Club sent to the Far East Games in Koshien. Members of the Nishinomiya Police Station, who were on guard, prevented them. In the ensuing struggle, the face and shoulder of Chief Investigator Kinoshita were lacerated. Swimmer Tetsuo Iyeshiro (Nihon University) suffered a right arm injury, and Toshihei Kaida of Tokyo Higher Normal School was injured in the face. Swimmers Tokushi Ishiharada (Meiji University) and Masanori Yusa (Nihon University), who rushed down from upstairs upon hearing the commotion, were injured in their arms. Yoshiyuki Kauchii (Waseda University) was also injured. Fortunately, the injuries to the athletes were not so severe as to prevent them from competing. The thugs were members of the Meisō Club Boxing Club in Iwabuchi, Tokyo.

(Electric News Agency, Koshien, 28th): The athletes sent to the Far East Games who were lodging in this Athlete's Hotel were demoralized by various acts of violence and agitation by a faction opposing participation. Despite concerns about their departure, they resolved to participate. At 9 AM this morning, they left the lodging and headed to Kobe to board the "Taihe Maru," which was waiting for them. They were escorted to Kobe by Hyogo Prefecture police in buses along the Hanshin National Highway. They boarded the "Taihe Maru" at noon.

Poor Track and Field Records (Electric News Agency, Osaka, 28th): The final record-keeping session for the track and field representatives to the Far East Games was held yesterday afternoon at the Koshien South Athletic Field under strict police guard. Except for the javelin throw of 65.50 meters by Saburo Nagao, there were no good records. This was partly due to the disputes surrounding participation, which affected the athletes' morale. Director Okita told reporters that the poor records were due to the athletes' mental state and that he believed they would recover before departure.

Central News Agency Sends Staff to the Philippines to Report on Far East Games; Feng Youzhen Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday and Set Sail in Two Days (Nanjing, 28th): The Far East Games are scheduled to be held in the Philippines on May 12th. The Central News Agency, recognizing the strong interest in sports among the Chinese people, is particularly concerned about this Games and has sent Chief Correspondent Feng Youzhen to the Philippines to transmit complete Games coverage. The news will then be broadcast nationwide by the headquarters. Feng arrived in Shanghai on the 28th and will set sail with the athlete delegation on the 2nd of next month.

Workers' Sports Meet Soccer News: Huadian Defeats Toothbrush 5-1; Today's Matches Postponed Due to Rain

The First City-Wide Workers' Sports Meet, organized by the Shanghai General Labor Union, held a soccer championship match yesterday afternoon at 3 PM at the China Soccer Field between the Huadian Labor Union and the Toothbrush Labor Union. Zhang Le served as the referee. Neither side scored in the first half. In the second half, Huadian's coordination improved, and their forwards scored five consecutive goals. With ten minutes left in the game, it started to rain, and Huadian scored an own goal. As a result, Huadian won 5-1. After the game, the rain became heavier, so all of today's soccer and basketball matches were postponed.
