Education News: Outlying Shaanxi Education Key Areas for Improvement Ministry of Education Supervisor's Report (Continued from Yesterday) As for "bad habits," in the past century, China has suffered from the invasion of foreign cultures, leading to the shaking and destruction of inherent Chinese etiquette. Meanwhile, the advantages of Western culture have not been successfully established. In this period of transition between the old and the new, a lawless society has formed, creating bad habits. All aspects of life, including clothing, food, housing, and transportation, lack proper restraint and have become a very loose way of life for the people. Due to bad habits, the spirit of the nation has declined daily. Especially since the "September 18th Incident" and the "January 28th Incident," people generally feel the invasion of imperialists, the danger to the country's status, and the lack of progress in Chinese politics. They believe that China is beyond saving and that it is best to live recklessly. With the loss of self-defense, general life has tended toward pessimism, negativity, romanticism, decadence, world-weariness, and hedonism. Society lacks discipline and order, so how can national spirit and national strength arise? "There is no greater sorrow than a dead heart." If the national psychology is so decadent, it will not be able to avoid destruction even without external troubles and internal worries, especially in these times of the strong preying on the weak. The influence of bad habits on society and the country is so great. There are many who talk about saving the country today, some say aviation will save the country, some say industry will save the country, some say domestic goods will save the country, etc. Although there are many methods, they are all biased towards one aspect and are not fundamental solutions. If the spirit of the nation is inclined towards negativity and decadence, how can any undertaking proceed? Therefore, the fundamental solution is to first invigorate the national spirit, and then all undertakings to save the country can be carried out. To restore the national spirit, we must first eliminate "bad habits," transform "old habits," and promote "new habits." Only then can we express a positive and upward spirit and promote all undertakings to save the country. Therefore, we see the order and restraint of the ancients and the lack of order and restraint of the moderns, and we see that the national crisis is worsening day by day. In order to think fundamentally, we have this New Life Movement.

10. The number of junior high school classes run by provincial normal schools is greater than the number of normal school classes, which goes against the original intention. From next year onwards, only normal school classes should be enrolled. If enrollment is difficult at present, a simplified normal course can be offered first. If there are junior high school classes, they can also be appropriately changed to simplified normal school classes.

11. The county normal schools in each county are all training courses for teachers, and the equipment, curriculum, and graduation period are not in line with regulations in many ways. Funding should be increased immediately, and they should be reorganized into simplified normal schools according to Article 6 of the Normal School Regulations.

12. The provincial vocational schools are few in number, and the results are not very impressive. In the future, in addition to thoroughly reorganizing the three existing schools, appropriate locations should be selected in the north and south, and junior and senior vocational schools should be added separately to meet local needs.

13. The workshops in each vocational school are not adequate. The internship time, except for the sewing, knitting, and dyeing departments of the Xi'an First Women's Public Vocational School, which already account for half of the teaching time, is far from the prescribed standards. They should be improved separately.

14. Women's secondary education in the province is quite backward. The number of schools should be increased according to plan, and the content should be enriched. In places where provincial women's secondary schools have not been established or cannot be added for a while, women's normal classes or women's middle school classes can be temporarily set up in provincial secondary schools to provide more opportunities for female primary school graduates to study.

15. The salaries of principals and directors of secondary schools should be divided into grades according to the number of classes and qualifications and experience. The teaching salaries of normal and vocational schools equivalent to senior high schools should also be paid according to senior high school standards to be fair. In addition, there are too many part-time teachers in each school, and the hours are fragmented. The full-time teacher system should be strictly implemented, and the number of part-time teachers should not exceed one-fourth of the total number of teachers.

16. The regulations for teacher training, salary scales, and annual salary increase regulations for secondary schools should be formulated as soon as possible and submitted to the Ministry for approval.

17. There are too many out-of-school children in the province. In addition to increasing the number of primary schools as much as possible, counties should be ordered to add simplified primary schools and short-term primary schools in accordance with Article 5 of the Primary School Regulations to promote free education.

18. The Department previously stipulated that all primary schools should start in the fall, which is not suitable for rural social life. Each school should be ordered to run spring classes to give more children the opportunity to attend school.

19. Many senior primary schools are still established independently in various counties. They should be ordered to add junior primary schools immediately or merge with other local junior primary schools to comply with the law.

20. The names of provincial and county primary schools should be corrected in accordance with Article 11 of the Primary School Regulations. Many primary schools in various counties still use the old model names. Their content is no different from ordinary primary schools. They should be ordered to abolish the word "model." It is also inappropriate for private groups to use public names for primary schools. In addition, the provincial experimental primary school lacks experimental plans and results and should be strictly reorganized to live up to its name.

21. The scores listed in the weekly teaching schedule for each subject in primary schools can be divided by three. The original intention was to facilitate the distribution of 30, 45, or 60 minutes into one class. Regardless of the subject, if 30 minutes are set as one class, it is too restrictive and loses the original meaning.

22. Primary school classes with fewer students should use a compound system in accordance with the Primary School Law to save expenses. The number of students in the lower grades is often excessive and the two-part system can be implemented to accommodate them.

23. The province is the source of Chinese culture, and the local teaching materials in various places are unusually rich. The education administrative agencies in each county should be ordered to be responsible for editing in accordance with Article 31 of the Primary School Regulations.

24. The teaching equipment of schools at all levels is extremely simple, except for a very small number. In the future, (1) public funds should be saved to support them, (2) equipment fees should be saved and used as a whole, (3) public science museums should be established in places with more schools, and (4) specimens, models, wall charts, and simple instruments should be made jointly by staff and students as much as possible.

25. Labor teaching should be thoroughly improved, and the religious curriculum of church schools should be completely abolished.

26. Many primary and secondary school teachers' teaching methods are inappropriate and urgently need to be studied and improved. The Primary School Education Research Association should also be organized in accordance with the Primary School Regulations.

27. After a strict reorganization, the order of general students is still good. However, in addition to negative sanctions and interference, more positive guidance and enlightenment should be added to achieve a more permanent effect of imperceptible influence.

28. The province's social education, in addition to the establishment of provincial institutions, is mostly poor in content and should be implemented in accordance with the proposed three-year social education plan to achieve results.

29. The province lacks social education talents and should attach a social education personnel training class to the provincial senior high school or the provincial first normal school. Each county should send personnel to receive training in stages. When the training is completed, they should be ordered to return to their place of origin to handle social education.

30. The province is the site of the capitals of the Zhou, Qin, Han, and Tang dynasties, and various antiquities, monuments, and documents are available everywhere. Destruction and dispersal are a pity. They should be transported in accordance with the implementation rules of the Law on the Preservation of Antiquities promulgated by the Executive Yuan and the revised organization outline of the Municipal and County Literature Committee, and the Antiquities Preservation Committee and the Literature Committee should be organized separately to be responsible for the collection and maintenance to respect antiquities.

Ministry of Education Orders Zhejiang, Shandong, and Jiangsu Education Departments to Implement Regional Guidance System and Distribute Guidance Outlines (Nanjing, 28th): The Ministry of Education ordered the Education Departments of Zhejiang, Shandong, and Jiangsu to investigate the general outline of the methods of regional guidance of county and municipal public education in each province, which had been resolved by the Ministry's Committee on Public Education and recorded and sent. The public education of counties and cities has always been promoted by the education departments of each province, but it is not easy to guide Zhou Min in each province, and progress is often slow. This regional guidance system can still remedy the above-mentioned malpractices and should be tried out first. It is found that the province can try out this system, and it is appropriate to copy and send the original resolution outline and order to follow it, formulate methods and submit them for approval. (1) The Provincial Education Department may divide the whole province into several public education guidance areas. (2) Each guidance area must set up a central guidance agency, which shall be designated by the Provincial Education Department from the provincial public education hall, experimental public school, or other equivalent provincial education agency in the province. (3) The powers of the district central guidance agency are as follows: 1. Supervise the promotion of public education in the whole area, 2. Guide the improvement of public education in the whole area, 3. Train public education service personnel in the area, 4. Organize experiments and demonstrations of public education. All public education institutions in the area shall accept the supervision and guidance of the district central guidance agency. The results of the supervision and guidance shall be assessed by the Education Department. The supervision and guidance plan of the District Central Guidance Agency shall be submitted to the Education Department for approval, and the progress of supervision and guidance shall be reported to the Education Department for record. (4) The district central guidance agency shall cooperate with the district party and government agencies, education agencies, autonomous agencies, education departments, and other relevant organizations and enthusiastic people. (5) The central guidance agency may organize a district public education research association. (6) All regulations on guidance shall be formulated by the education departments of each province and reported to the Ministry of Education for approval.

University Presidents Must Not Hold Concurrent Positions (Nanjing, 28th): The National Government issued an order on the 28th to amend and promulgate Article 9 of the University Organization Law. The article is as follows: A university shall have a president who shall be responsible for all university affairs. The presidents of national, provincial, and municipal universities shall be appointed to a simple position and shall not hold other positions except for teaching courses at the university.

Education Bureau Orders Colleges and Universities to Postpone Enrollment to August

The Municipal Education Bureau instructed the private colleges and universities in the city yesterday: It is hereby ordered that the new students enrolled by colleges and universities should be held in late July at the earliest, which has been communicated to the Ministry for compliance. Now, due to the complex procedures of the education departments of provinces and cities for handling the unified examination and issuing certificates, the date of enrollment is still not conducive to students' further education. Therefore, it is specially re-ordered that the new students enrolled by colleges and universities should be postponed to August. In addition to separate lines, it is appropriate to order the Bureau to instruct compliance.

Student Unrest in the Third Grade of Songjiang Provincial High School (Songjiang News): Students in the third grade of Songjiang Provincial High School have been brewing student unrest recently, and it broke out yesterday. Three probation students, Tang Zeyi, Shen Runmin, and Huang Zhaoguang, have been expelled by the principal for destroying the school badge, a serious offense, in accordance with the Jiangsu Education Department's Order No. 252 on rectifying the school spirit. The families of the other students in the class have been sent letters to persuade their children to come to school, stating that the students have been studying for nearly three years, and that when the summer vacation comes, they should work hard to complete their studies to live up to the expectations of their parents. Now, they still do not ask whether it is right or wrong, do not consider the pros and cons, and do not talk about reason. It is clear that they are motivated by temporary emotions and are actually obstructing the holding of the mid-term examination. Therefore, there are requests to withdraw from school and arbitrary strikes. Persuasion is ineffective, and the school authorities are heartbroken. They hope that the students will achieve success and are willing to compromise. They are hereby requested to persuade their children to come to school. It is reported that the reason for this student unrest is that the graduation examination will be held in Zhenjiang in accordance with the regulations. The school authorities plan to hold a mid-term examination before going to the provincial capital for the examination to select students who have completed their studies and whose examination results are acceptable to participate in the provincial examination. The students believe that the mid-term examination is redundant and are unwilling to comply with it. This is one reason. One night, some students went out of the school privately, and a director saw it. He did not stop them at the time and told the principal afterwards, who expelled and recorded the students. The students are dissatisfied. Recently, an mimeographed publication of Lao Yingji was found, with satirical articles. It was bound at Dashengchang yesterday and was found by the school. The Public Security Bureau was asked to send someone to Dashengchang to search for it and summon student Dai Kunpei for questioning. This is another reason. The school has scheduled to hold a spring sports meet, and the third grade students have agreed not to participate. It is said that Principal Peng Weiji is determined to rectify the school spirit. The two sides have different opinions. I wonder how the final result will be resolved.

Shanghai Social Education Society Holds Inaugural Meeting Today at 2 PM at the Citizen Education Hall; Pan Gongzhan and others Elected as Presidium Members. The Shanghai Social Education Society was initiated and organized by the social education community in Shanghai last year. Now the preparations have been completed, and the number of members has reached more than 150. The Eleventh Issue of Women's Garden: The End of Eugenics by Xu Xizhen

On the road of modern cultural development, World War I clearly became an indelible milestone. Besides exposing the faces of the rulers, the lesson it taught people was the awakening of scholars in general to the conflict between theory and fact. After the World War, the development of capitalism proceeded at a high speed, and its end - the coming of economic collapse - also took on a rapidly declining trend. The general theoretical doctrines before the war also got an opportunity to be practically tested, and eugenics was one of them.

The sole purpose of eugenics is to attempt to improve the race based on biological principles. They treat the race with Darwin's law of elimination and selection, and believe that the family is the social organization that has a direct relationship with the race. Therefore, eugenicists have put as much effort into family issues as sociologists: they believe that the family is the unit of society, mainly because it has the function of reproduction. They believe that the disintegration of modern family organization is a terrible morbidity. They oppose the combination of men and women who do not engage in reproductive function. They oppose women engaging in social movements (they say that even if women's movements are necessary, they should only be done by a few women who lack "motherhood"; but this is actually equivalent to opposition, because is the so-called "women's movement" not the business of a "small number of women"?). They believe that a woman's natural duty is to be a virtuous child-rearing woman, or the generally so-called "virtuous wife and good mother," to make a contribution to the cause of improving the race. On the one hand, they oppose the romantic spirit of individualism, and on the other hand, they criticize the socialist public child-rearing. Starting from eugenics, these conclusions are naturally not surprising. From the perspective of improving the race, what else can women do besides being virtuous mothers? It is simply a tedious task to explain or deny the above proposition; for example, to try to explain the pros and cons of public child-rearing, the necessity for women to engage in the acquisition of a reasonable social system, etc., are the work of experts. At the same time, we don't want to use some socialist jargons or even maliciously criticize the fallacies of eugenicists. We only want to use the facts of the current society to illustrate whether the natural duty of women is limited to "raising good babies" and whether such designs can exist at all.

First, let's take a look at countries where capitalism is more developed; before and after the war, under the tense situation, everyone wanted to find a new stimulus, and individualistic conscious elements sneaked into literature and sociology. The pursuit of pleasure, accompanied by the special national character of loving freedom, made the family organization in the society increasingly unstable. The interest in this phenomenon is of course not sudden. When the method of production reached the stage of the industrial revolution, the organization of the family also began to gradually disintegrate. This is a phenomenon that eugenicists are very worried about. Women of the laboring class threw away the "natural duty" of child-rearing or household chores and ran into factories, working with gears and motors. Intellectual women of the propertied class are no longer happy to be bothered by children. People regard children as a hateful burden for the sake of life and enjoyment, but at that time it was only "hateful." What about now when capitalism is collapsing? Children are wanted, but the lack of the ability to raise them is a fact. We run into the magnificent cities of the gold standard countries. You can go and see how many men's hearts are beating in the reception room of the obstetrics hospital every day, "Damn, what terrible children."

In China, the concept of family is more intense than in any other country. According to the usual practice, it seems that there is no need for eugenicists to worry and teach the inherent duty of child-rearing. But what is the current situation? A small part (a very small part) of educated people are infected with the atmosphere of individualism and are unwilling to have children. Most of the petty citizens who have been formally brainwashed by the ancient訓of "There are three unfilial acts" are mostly willing to have children, but "giving birth" is done, but "raising" becomes a big problem. The result is that the society adds a group of "half-baked" people. As for the working class and peasants? In a straightforward sentence: "We can't afford to raise sons!" After a woman gives birth to a child, she thinks it is an excellent opportunity and throws her son to a mansion to be a nanny. For this, they are not completely unaware of any shortcomings. They also resent their own lack of ability. The harsh treatment of pregnant women in factories makes them feel at all times: "This world is a bit wrong."

It's not that they don't want a family; it's that they can't maintain it. What should they do? The profound theories and worries of eugenics are of no use to them. Even if they are willing to be "virtuous wives and good mothers," reality makes them doubt. Under such circumstances, the more prosperous the population productivity, the more anemic, weak, and ignorant people there will be in the society, and the consequences will of course be unimaginable.

New women under a reasonable social system will certainly not be the "good child-rearing women" ideal of eugenicists, and their labor will not only be spent on lullabies and breastfeeding. If the social system is as chaotic as it is now, how can "eugenics" be "good"?

For this, eugenicists will definitely say, "That's not our business," but because those scholars have neglected the economic organization as the foundation of society, the "peaceful world" in the imagination of eugenicists has always become the ideal country of the twentieth century.

The fact is that women in the new era will not (or can be said to be unable to) stay at home to do child-rearing work. We believe that only in this way can we approach a reasonable social system.

World Great Thinkers' Opinions on Women's Issues (4) by Hua

John Stuart Mill John Stuart Mill (John Stuart Mill) was born in 1806 and died in 1873. He was a great British philosopher, political activist, and economist of the time. His father, James Mill, was an authority on classical economics - one of the famous students of Ricardo. Therefore, the young Mill, inheriting the legacy of his ancestors, was also one of the representatives of the era when classical economics was declining. He wrote a book "Principles of Political Economy," which summarized and systematized the economic thoughts popular in Britain in the first half of the nineteenth century.

John Stuart Mill was also one of the first to advocate women's equality. In 1870, he published his famous book "The Subjection of Women," which was widely popular. In this book, he first reasoned from the perspective of social development that women must be in a position of equality with men. He said: "If people think that the theory of equality between the sexes is only based on theory; then it should be remembered that the theory of inequality between the sexes, in addition to theory, has no other reason. All practical experience proves that the theory of equality between the sexes is beneficial, which is nothing more than saying that mankind can only survive under this system (equality between men and women), to this day we have seen this stage of progress and happiness. ······Experience certainly proves that with each month of improvement, the social status of women will be raised one step. Historians and philosophers must use the increase or decrease of the social status of women as the most accurate and appropriate measure of the civilization of a nation or a century. If we try to review all eras of human history, we can see that the status of women is constantly approaching equality with men. This alone, although not sufficient to prove that this movement must reach full equality, is undoubtedly some inferential data: the fact is indeed so." To this day, some people who oppose women's liberation, their main argument is that women's innate qualities are fundamentally inferior to men's, meaning that women are born as "inferior races" and should not be equal to men. In fact, this view is still a traditional fallacy. John Stuart Mill said long ago: "The most stubborn and persistent people who scold women dare not deny that women - if we add together the modern experience and the experience of the past centuries, it can be said that not a few women, but most women - can do everything that men can do, and they do it very smoothly and sincerely. The most important thing is that there are many events that no woman has successfully done as well as some - very few - men, and there are some things that they have not yet reached the highest stage of perfection. Is it not obvious that prohibiting women from competing with men in some similar occupations is a great infringement on women's rights and a great loss to society?······Oral Hygiene for Children by You Bai

The mouth is the gateway for food to enter the body. If the mouth is not washed and the teeth are not brushed, various germs can be swallowed into the stomach and intestines with food and drink without intention, causing infection and illness. Moreover, the residue of food and dirt adheres to the inside and outside of the teeth, slowly causing inflammation of the gums, or viruses invading the dental pulp, causing pulpitis. Good teeth become bad teeth. Initially, chewing is inconvenient, and toothache often occurs, causing nervousness. Then, various gastrointestinal diseases occur, and as a result, the development of the whole body is hindered. Especially in childhood, the stomach and intestines are weak and development is incomplete, so the harm is even easier to occur.

From the above, oral hygiene is so closely related to children's health. Then all parents and teachers who are responsible for raising and educating children must cultivate children's oral hygiene habits. The simplest and easiest methods are as follows: (1) Brush your teeth twice every morning and evening, and wash and dry the toothbrush. (2) Rinse your mouth after meals. (3) Eat less candy, especially dates. (Eating too much can easily damage the enamel.) (4) Do not chew hard objects. (5) Do not eat things that are too cold or too hot. (6) Do not put your fingers or sharp penholders into your mouth. (7) Do not pick your teeth with fingernails or other unclean things.

When parents and teachers find that children's teeth are deformed, overlap, or have decayed teeth, they should go to a dentist for correction and treatment, so that their teeth can develop normally, maintain the proper development of the whole body, and cultivate a healthy and happy little citizen - the future master of China.

Overseas Women's News by Biwu

(1) International Open Door Federation (Open Door International) The International Open Door Federation is composed of women representatives from eighteen countries. The third conference will be held in Belgrade, the capital of Yugoslavia, on January 5th of this year. More than 80 representatives will attend to discuss issues such as women's employment, labor of married women, women's physical labor, etc., and unanimously resolved to oppose all restrictions imposed on these issues.

(2) International Equal Rights Alliance (Equal Rights International) The fifth conference of the International Equal Rights Alliance was held in Geneva last December, with participants from 22 countries. The International Open Door Federation and the American Women's Federation have joined. The purpose of the association was to obtain equal rights for men and women. Now it has slightly changed, and it will devote all its efforts to concluding international treaties on equality between men and women. Its thoughts and actions are roughly the same as those of the American Women's Federation.

(3) Pacific Women's Conference The Pacific Women's Conference is composed of women representatives from countries along the Pacific coast and the United Kingdom and India related to it, totaling thirteen countries. It is scheduled to hold a conference in Honolulu in August of this year, with a session of about one month. Its main topics are: labor women and family issues, women and international peace, women's trafficking, children and mothers' health issues, women's political participation issues, vocational education issues, etc.

(4) Victory of Women at the Pan-American Conference From December 3rd to 26th last year, the Seventh Pan-American Conference was held in Montevideo, Uruguay. At that time, two major proposals were put forward regarding women, one: "Equality between men and women in nationality law," and the other: "Equality between men and women in politics and law in all countries participating in this conference." The two proposals were rejected by a small margin: the first proposal has been passed. Previously, a similar proposal to the first proposal was submitted at the Hague International Law Codification Conference hosted by the League of Nations. Although women tried their best at that time, it ended in failure. Therefore, the success of the Pan-American Conference can be said to be the honor of women in the New World.

(5) Peruvian Women's Election Movement Begins South American countries are extremely depressed in the women's movement due to the influence of their mother country. Recently, due to the Spanish Revolution, the autocratic monarchs were driven away, and the people's spirit gradually expanded. Therefore, women in South American countries have gradually shown vitality. Many well-known women in Lima, the capital of Peru, saw the victory of women at the Montevideo Pan-American Conference. Therefore, a meeting was held to decide to carry out a women's election movement.

(6) Portugal stipulates the qualifications for women's suffrage Since the revolution, Portugal has given women the right to participate in politics, but there are some restrictions on the qualifications, namely: (1) Those who have the right to vote in district councils - widows, divorced women, separated women, and single women who have the responsibility of supporting the elderly and young. (2) Those who have the right to vote in local councils - men must be able to read and write and pay taxes. Women must have received secondary and higher education or hold public office. (3) Those who have the right to vote in the Central Council and the President - those who have the right to vote in local councils.

(7) The misfortunes of German women under Hitler's rule It is well known that German women have suffered great misfortunes since Hitler's dictatorship came to power. It began with a strange cry that "women should belong to the family!" and exempted many women officials or teachers from their positions. Then, the right of married women to be employed was restricted. In December last year, there was also an agreement to exclude female doctors at the meeting of the government and medical groups. This year, the government stipulates that the national university enrollment quota is 15,000, and only 1,500 women are allowed, accounting for one-tenth of the total. Moreover, the entrance examinations for women are made difficult in many ways. In addition to academic ability, there must also be a physical and personal examination.

Mother's Heart by Liang - A Page of Diary -

The rumbling of cars on the street shattered my good dream. In a daze, I saw the sunlight sneaking in through the cracks in the window, telling me the time, telling me that it was not early. Still, I was attacked by fatigue, and for the sake of work and life, I had to support myself to get up. Looking at Man'er, who was sleeping soundly in the bed, her cheeks were as red as ripe apples, her dry lips had several cracks, and her eyelids were swollen. This was the result of last night's crying. The child who always smiles, everyone says is cute, cried and fussed like this last night. Needless to say, the burning heat was enough to make her suffer. But I was tired and eager to rest, how impatiently I scolded her, how cruel I am, "Mom" I am ashamed. After dressing Hui'er, washing her face, and preparing breakfast, I also tidied up hastily, filled my stomach, and it was already half past eight. I told Wang Ma (she is the only person I entrust when I go out to work) how to take care of Man'er as usual, and asked her to pay special attention to her cold and warmth, and diet, because her fever had not completely subsided. In this way, I took Hui'er and hurried out the door. Six-year-old Hui'er has a curious and active nature, and there is simply no moment of stillness. She doesn't understand danger, doesn't know the harm, tries this, takes that, it is indeed the most difficult to manage and most needs to be educated period for children. Fortunately, he and I are in the same school, and I can take care of his actions from time to time, otherwise, I don't know how I will worry about him? There are four lessons today, which is really not too busy. Because I am afraid that I will not have time after returning home, the distribution of teaching materials, the collection of references, and the correction of test papers completely filled the empty time. But because of the sleeplessness at night and Man'er's illness, I was absent-minded and could not concentrate on my work. The day before yesterday, Director Chen told me that the cleanliness and order of my class have greatly deteriorated recently, and this time the arithmetic competition was at the bottom again. His words contained a warning meaning, which I felt. I was also a competitive person, and it was not that I didn't want to be outstanding in everything, but the environment was always so difficult. My body, since giving birth to two children, has neither been properly recuperated nor had adequate rest, and it is very different from the past. Recently, because of the busy work, I feel even more exhausted. If this continues, not to mention that the school will be dissatisfied with me, I myself feel that it is difficult to cope with. But when I think about it, will the panic of unemployment not aggravate the mental pain? I can only do it, and work hard!

The last bell rang, and I was as if I had been pardoned - this is not because I am not loyal to my work, Man'er's illness really occupies my whole heart - I took Hui'er home. Entering the door, after receiving her from Wang Ma's hand, half of the heavy burden on my heart has been lifted, because from her face and forehead, I know that the situation is not as bad as I expected in the school. In my series of questions: "Did she cry?" "Did she eat porridge?" "How many times?" "How much?" "How long did she sleep?" "How are the bowel movements?" "When did the fever completely subside?" Wang Ma's answers made me feel satisfied. The worries disappeared temporarily like smoke. Jian came back and saw a smile on the corner of Man'er's mouth. She unfolded the clouds of sorrow on her face and forced a smile to say to me: "With a mother like you, the children will not suffer too much." Is this comforting me? On the contrary, it made me uneasy. A mother with weak ability has tried her best to fight for life. Although the happiness of the children is the only wish that surrounds her heart, she still cannot help but neglect it due to the limitations of time and energy. The reason is not that she doesn't love her children, but that she loves them too much. Dinner was earlier than usual. As usual, I warmed up Hui'er's homework and took care of some chores. After settling the two children to sleep, I also wanted to rest. After getting into bed, the fatigue of the body had reached its peak, but the brain still did not listen to commands and kept turning, from the health of the children to the education of the children, the future, the responsibilities and burdens of the parents, the occupation and life!! Gradually, in many blurry images, I lost consciousness.

After Marriage (Continued) by Lian Sheng

Although we are poor, we can live comfortably every month by selling articles to maintain our lives. We live in the pavilion room - bedroom, kitchen, reception room, dining room. Although I grew up in the life of the aristocracy, everything I used to disdain to do, I am now doing happily one by one, without complaining or worrying. This surprised his friends. Before, they only thought that I was just a beautiful and modern college student. Naturally, household chores were something I disdained to do. But the fact is the opposite. Every day, I go to the vegetable market to buy vegetables, cook side dishes, cook rice, wash dishes, wash clothes, sweep the floor, mop the floor····Who says it doesn't make them sigh, even their wives from the countryside are unwilling to buy side dishes! I wanted to find a job, but he wouldn't allow it. He said: What do women do, they are just vases for the institution! Taking a step back, I said to seek a teacher's position, but he also disagreed, because this would give other men a chance to please me. What can I do? I have to listen to him, otherwise, our feelings will break down because of this. I can only bury myself in writing articles, and he approves of this. I have a child in my stomach, and I am already seven months pregnant. Sometimes when we argue over a small matter, he will say that the child is not his. "Let's see when it is born. If it doesn't look like me, it is not my child!" What arbitrary words. I don't know how many tears I have shed in secret for these words. Really, what method can I use to explain? And who can guarantee that the child born in the future will really look like him? This injustice will always be buried in my heart.

Because of his narrow-mindedness, after marriage, I cut off relations and correspondence with my former boyfriend - unless he is his friend. I dare not mention any of their names, as this would make him jealous and hate me. Although it is said that this is his expression of love for me, I only feel that it restricts my freedom too much. Even my former male classmates dare not pay attention to me when we meet - alas! I feel that he is too selfish!

The whole morning is his time to write articles. Naturally, I dare not say a word to him. I drag my heavy belly and wash vegetables and cook rice downstairs back and forth. Sometimes, if the taste of the vegetables is slightly bad, he will complain, and he will not be considerate of you at all. Often I can't eat at all and I am full of grievances. But he still has to say: Go home, it's good to be a young lady at home, no one scolds you. Here, of course I will scold you if you do something wrong. I don't care, who else will care about you? What kind of words are these that make people feel so painful? And how discouraging they are! The spring is bright and the spring air is rippling on the earth, making people feel relaxed and intoxicated. At this time, he could no longer be confined in the pavilion room. He proposed to travel to the West Lake. Of course, I, who am about to give birth, should not move too much. I can only persuade him to go by himself, and I can take good care of myself. He was worried about me, so he didn't mention going again! However, when he is bored in the room, he will say that I am too involved with him and not giving him a chance to relax - alas! How cruel he is to say such words. I can only give him a bitter smile. Really, my heart has been broken into pieces! Now, he is shouting for divorce every day. May 1st is our wedding anniversary, and we agreed to separate on that day, which is actually divorce. He said he wouldn't care about the child, and I could do whatever I wanted with it. "What about the production fee?" "I'll leave you a hundred yuan," he said. Alas! I have nothing to say. This is what life is like after marriage! (To be continued)

Reading Introduction Ten Lectures on Women's Issues by Ziwen

Written by Hisao Honma, translated by Xi Chen Zhang, published by Kaiming Bookstore, 1.5 yuan. Women have always been in the position of "being made," but the progress of the times does not allow this to exist forever. Therefore, the issue of women has become an important issue in transforming the current society. The original work is by a Japanese scholar with comparative practical learning, and the translation is also very smooth. The book has a total of ten lectures, with sophisticated discussions on the origin and significance of the women's movement, love, marriage, divorce, and other issues. It can also be said to be a preliminary textbook for the women's movement. The translator's attached "The Intellectual Development of Chinese Women" is also included. It gives a detailed description of the misfortunes of Chinese women in the past, as well as the recent liberation movement.

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly Amateur Talks: Our Understanding of Local Autonomy by Gongpu

Since the reporter has repeatedly written articles discussing the Shanghai municipal election, it has recently attracted the attention of all parties, which is very gratifying. However, there are several opinions that should be explained: First, some people think that paying attention to the concession area is too narrow. Of course, when discussing the election and the issue of Chinese representatives in the Shanghai municipal election, the minimum is to hope for the progress of Shanghai's municipality and the improvement of election methods. However, the reporter's purpose in making such a discussion is not limited to the corner of Shanghai, nor is it specifically referring to the Public Concession in Shanghai, which has complex international relations. However, the purpose is to use this municipal system with a considerable history as a basis for discussion, to encourage citizens' interest in the municipality, actively participate in the election, and further pay attention to national politics, so as to reduce obstacles to the future of democratic politics. Now the draft constitution has been promulgated. Many people in the country have made theoretical explorations on this brilliant national fundamental law, but if it only stops at research, it will not be of much benefit to the future of constitutional implementation. On the one hand, we hope that the country will have a good fundamental law, and the protection of civil rights can be established, but we also hope that the law is not a dead letter, but can be thoroughly realized in practice. Therefore, it is important to study the advantages and disadvantages of the constitution, but it is equally important to consider the gradual implementation methods in practice, otherwise the constitution will naturally become a dead letter and lose its spirit. We start from the municipal aspect to discuss the issue of elections. The purpose is to practically explore gradual implementation methods, because municipal issues are more closely related to citizens and are more likely to arouse citizens' attention and interest; at the same time, we also know that the implementation of a constitutional system in a country must start from one place.

Some people also say that now the general public can be said to be holding a kind of aversion, despair, negativity, and indifference to politics, thinking that there is no future for politics in our country. Of course, the pitch-black politics of the past 20 years can indeed make people pessimistic, and various high-profile reforms of politics have also been sung enough, but so far none of them have been realized. In this environment, the general lack of political interest, and the inherently weak political understanding of the Chinese people, it is not surprising that they not only dare not hold any attempts to improve politics, but are full of hatred and disgust. In addition, people below the middle class in the current society are all feeling the pressure of difficult life and the threat of unemployment and poverty. Therefore, the general public is busy trying to make a profit and solve the problem of food and clothing, so how can they have the leisure to care about politics! If this kind of mentality is not broken, it will only make politics worse, more unbearable, and more difficult to reform, until the country is destroyed. In the first article discussing the Shanghai municipality, the reporter quoted what Mr. Meng said that the Shanghai concession municipality was controlled by a small number of privileged classes, and strongly said that the reason for this phenomenon was that the citizens were too indifferent to politics. Therefore, if we want to improve the status quo, we should thoroughly eradicate the previous negative attitude and pessimistic psychology towards the Shanghai municipality, and replace it with a constructive spirit of actively seeking improvement methods.

The third opinion is that some people think that civic training is not easy to be effective under the current situation. Everyone knows that political reform cannot be achieved overnight. It must go through countless trials, improvements, and evolutions before there can be hope for gradual clarity. Take the United Kingdom as an example, although it is the most developed country in the constitutional system and its parliamentary politics are envied by the world, the fact is that its political shortcomings are still everywhere. But even this kind of politics cannot be achieved immediately. It has gone through a process of nearly 300 years of trial and improvement, and even had bloody revolutions at the beginning. Therefore, we must have a strong interest in studying politics and a enthusiastic courage to participate in politics. We must not be easily disappointed, nor should we have excessive expectations, hoping to reach the sky in one step.

We certainly hope that the public should have a long-term vision in political ideals, and everyone should actively discuss and study the gains and losses of political systems, but in the actual improvement of politics, we hope that the people can think about it from small things and gradually seek improvement methods. We should first start with the municipal reform of one place and then extend to the renewal of national politics. Although the constitution has not been implemented, local autonomy has been earnestly implemented by the central government in various provinces and cities. However, this important work does not seem to have been actively promoted in various provinces and cities. Their reason is that everything is unstable and there is no time to take care of it. But what about the achievements of local autonomy in more stable provinces such as Jiangsu and Zhejiang? This is really something they cannot explain. We must understand that local autonomy is the foundation for realizing democracy. Without the thorough realization of local autonomy, it is impossible to talk about constitutionalism. We should not blame the inefficiency of the government's work, but first blame ourselves for being too indifferent to the importance of local autonomy and too lacking in the ability to supervise the government. We should deeply realize that if the people completely rely on the government, cannot supervise it, and do not have the ability to exercise civil rights, then even if there are wise rulers, they will slowly become corrupt. Just look at the fact that even the autonomy of one county or city in China is not well done, so how can we talk about national democracy?

Life Sitting Surrounded by Books by Jixin - The Life of a Librarian -

The place where I live now is like a pigeon cage. "Book City," I find it funny when I think of this name. I give credit to those people who can have the leisure and time to think of this nice-sounding name. I am indeed sitting surrounded by books now, but my soul does not need such towering walls to protect it.

Walking into the door, there is an unbearable smell that rushes into your nostrils. A small rectangular room is divided into two parts. One side is the library, and I am locked in this place. One side is the reading room, which is for students to read books. There is a door in the middle that can be passed through. A four-foot-high cabinet is installed near the entrance. I stand inside the cabinet, just like a shop assistant. The customers who come here every day are all university students in the school. Rather than saying that these customers are more refined, it is better to say that these customers are more difficult to deal with.

Although my work is said to be only six hours, it is actually endless and can never be finished. From 1 pm to 5 pm, and from 7 pm to 9 pm, I have to serve to borrow books. Because of the restrictions in the rules, each person can only borrow one book at a time. Some people who are writing papers look at a dozen books in an hour. On normal days, there are fewer people reading books. When it comes to exams, this room is crowded with people. On average, these days account for the majority. So after the bell rings, in these few hours, I am always mindlessly drilling around in this pile of books. Especially at night, because of the stimulation of the intensity of the light, coupled with the daytime fatigue, even if a book is standing in front of me, I have to repeat it several times before I can distinguish it.

If I don't explain it in detail, you may think that I can still study on my own in the morning, but in fact the work in the morning is even more complicated. Every morning and afternoon, the tea room will send two packages from the post office. They are all bundles of books and newspapers; big and small, from institutions and schools, they have to be unpacked, the curled ones are pressed flat, and then the card boxes are taken to register them. Many new ones have to be divided into categories according to their nature. Sometimes, because Mr. Director wants to do extensive research, he runs to the old bookstore and buys many books by the pound and load, and puts them on the floor like a small pile of mountains. These endless burdens are all placed on my shoulders.

In such a place, using these times, doing this kind of work, who can not feel dry and tired? And how can I have the mood and leisure to enjoy myself?

Speaking of the treatment, it is also laughable. In terms of qualifications, I am certainly not comparable. Most of them here have at least a bachelor's degree, and some have even drunk foreign water. The working hours are the same, but the salaries they get are different. Some have twice as high as the low ones, or even three times as high. Some get ninety yuan, some get forty-five yuan, and some get thirty yuan. I am one of them. But I don't feel wronged, because there are also people with a bachelor's degree who get thirty yuan. There are even people with higher salaries who do less work. There is an Englishman who gets ninety yuan a month and only needs to work three hours a day. I don't know how this standard of treatment is set. The common saying, of course, is attributed to their knowledge - saying qualifications may be more accurate. But knowledge is not a glorious thing, if you have money to send your children to school, unless they are morons, I think anyone can do what they do.

Scientific Talks: Sunlight Machine by Tianhua

The Soviet Union has been engaged in the research on the utilization of solar energy (Sun energy) for a long time. In the Institute of Physics in Tashkent (in Central Asia, very close to Shule City in Xinjiang, China), through the efforts of scientists Cao Feimov and Fa Deyev, this knowledge has gradually been applied to daily practical life. In cold weather, using the glare machine they invented can keep the room temperature at 80 degrees; it can also be used for cooking, boiling soup, and brewing tea. In hot weather, through its sophisticated mechanism, the indoor air can be kept fresh and cool without change.

A simple sunlight machine is placed on the tail top. It rotates towards the sun. In this way, the solar energy collected in the machine is transmitted to the room for heating water, boiling eggs, warming the house and other tasks. Here, some skeptics may ask, what if there is a cloudy rainy day? There is no need to worry about this. The sunlight machine not only "collects" solar energy, but also "stores" solar energy for emergencies on cloudy and rainy days.

In winter, it may sound a little strange, the sunlight machine will store solar energy more efficiently than in the hot summer. This is because the sun's rays are purer (Purer) in winter.

Houses equipped with this type of sunlight machine are even more needed near the distant Arctic Ocean. The sun does not warm the ground in these cold places, but with the sunlight machine, it will warm the houses for the residents of these places. Solar energy can also be transmitted, for example, through underground pipes, it will not take much time to send it to the White Sea coast.

The utilization of solar energy is also extremely cost-effective. The sunlight machine described above costs only twenty to thirty rubles per unit.

Until now, the sunlight machine is still in the experimental stage. Although eight units have been applied and the performance is very good, the inventors are still unwilling to say that their efforts have achieved satisfactory results. However, they have explained to people with a determined attitude that in the near future, every household will have a sunlight machine on their roof, just like we now have a window or a door on the wall of our house.

This research is still being carried out in Tashkent, Uzbekistan (Central Asia). It seems to be a fantasy - to achieve such success without using many complex machines; but the fact is placed in front of us.

According to a report by Reuters on the 17th of this month, the final settlement of the British fiscal year in 1933 was: income of 72

Document Presented to the Municipal Government 156

A document presented regarding the issuance of a proclamation by your esteemed government to resolve disputes over rice transportation, implement measures, address the current difficult situation, considering the financial burden of businesses, requesting postponement of implementation, and seeking compassion. It is with utmost respect that we read in various newspapers in this city on the 24th of this month, your esteemed government's proclamation regarding the dispute over rice transportation at the Zhabei rice market wharf. Now, based on the Social Affairs Bureau's continued submission, there are seven implementation measures to be proclaimed and ordered for compliance. The gist of the measures is to allocate welfare funds for workers from the original wages. The shortfall resulting from the allocation will be provided by the firms to the workers. In other words, the firms must bear the welfare expenses in addition to the original wages, which is extremely thoughtful for the workers. If the firms can afford it, there would be no objection. However, in the current social climate, everyone is deeply troubled. Since the January 28th Incident, firms have been closing down one after another. Those who have managed to survive are struggling to stay afloat. Encountering this misfortune, reviving and revitalizing the economy requires a comprehensive approach that considers both industry and commerce. Using this to benefit workers is akin to treating a boil by cutting away flesh. The firms cannot afford it, and the situation is unbearable. Moreover, the incident stems from the Shi Deng Society inciting a crowd to rob and seize rice transport, which is purely an act of external parties encroaching on the workers of the firms. Among the workers themselves, there is mutual understanding and harmony between labor and capital in this precarious situation. Therefore, the so-called welfare issue today is a problem arising as a consequence of the Shi Deng Society's robbery. It is clear that if the Shi Deng Society's robbery is deemed an illegal act, then the welfare issue arising as a consequence of the robbery cannot be tolerated or acknowledged. To tolerate or acknowledge this would be akin to advocating for illegal workers, and if such news spreads, all legitimate merchants will feel threatened. Furthermore, this welfare issue was not involved at the beginning of the case. Even in the four measures issued by the Social Affairs Bureau on January 5th regarding the resolution of disputes over rice transportation at the rice market wharf along the Wusong River, there was not a single word about this issue. It was not until the meeting convened on February 8th that it was mentioned. Since the association and others felt that commerce was declining and they were ultimately unable to cope, they never expressed approval. Moreover, on March 19th, they outlined the reasons why they could not bear the welfare expenses in a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, requesting the Social Affairs Bureau to maintain the status quo, which is on record. Now, the Social Affairs Bureau is submitting to your esteemed government, claiming that it has obtained the consent of all parties, believing that the additional wages paid to the foremen are minimal and not difficult to bear, and requesting the issuance of a proclamation for compliance. Forcing people to do what they cannot do and compelling people to do what is difficult, the association and others in the same industry are truly fearful when considering the past and the future. Therefore, we do not hesitate to risk offense and lay out our grievances, requesting your esteemed leader to examine and consider the difficulties of merchants, and to grant a temporary postponement of the implementation of the aforementioned seven measures. Otherwise, the association and others in the same industry will be forced by livelihood and find it impossible to bear. Respectfully presented to the Mayor of Shanghai, Wu. Grain and Bean Industry Association Chairman Gu Xinyi, Rice Milling Industry Association Chairman Zhu Zixiang, Marketing Industry Association Chairman Zhang Songtao. Respectfully presented.

Cold Spring Harms Jiangzhe Silkworm Season 157

A Central News Agency report states that recent reports from Jiangzhe indicate damage to silkworms due to spring rains, resulting in illness, with silkworms unable to wake from their sleep and displaying symptoms of black spots and yellow discharge. Yesterday morning, the reporter met with He Shangping, head of the Shanghai liaison office of the National Economic Commission's Silkworm Improvement Association, who stated that due to the colder weather this spring, mulberry trees budded later, so the hatching of improved silkworm eggs was also later than in previous years. Currently, only a small portion of improved eggs have been hatched, and the results are excellent. As for local silkworms, because artificial suppression cannot be applied, some of the earlier hatched silkworms have suffered losses, but not to the extent of the various rumors.
